 bharat or bangladesh ke bich fatullah main khele ja rahe test muqaabale kaa pehla din agar shikhar dhawan ke naam rahaa, to tisare din ke hero murali vijay rahe
 Murali Vijay played an innings of 150 runs in the rain affected area
 isse pehle shikhar dhawan ne 173 ran banaae the
 This is the second time in Test cricket, when Shikhar Dhawan and Murali Vijay have scored 150 or more runs in a single innings
 isse pehle march, 2013 main mohali main khele gaye australia ke khilaaf test match main shikhar dhawan ne 187 or murali vijay ne 153 ran kii pari kheli thi
 The pair is only the third such pair in cricket history to have scored more than 150-150 runs in a single innings
 in donon ke atirikt srilanka ke marvan attapattu or sanath jayasoorya tathaa dakshin africa kii grem smith or harshal gibs kii jodi ye karnama do-do baar dikhaa chuki he
 However, Shikhar Dhawan and Murali Vijay are the second such pair of India, who have scored more than 150 runs in a single innings
 dhawan or vijay se pehle vinu macond or pranoy roy kii jodi ne 1956 main ek hi pari main kramash: 231 or 173 ran banaae the
 Apart from these two, Sri Lanka's Mervan Attapattu and Sanath Jayasuriya and South Africa's Graeme Smith and Herschelle Gibbs have shown this feat twice
 vaise shikhar dhawan or murali vijay bharat kii duusari aisi jodi he, jisane ek hi pari main 150 se zyada ran banaae hai
 Prior to Dhawan and Vijay, the pair of Veenu Makand and Prannoy Roy had scored 231 and 173 runs in the same innings in 1956
 marathavada main jaalnaa jile ke ek gaanv main karj main duube 40 varshiya ek kisaan ne jab graminon ko apane 'antim sanskaar' ke liye 'nimantran' diya to logon ko is baat kaa andaja bhi nahin hoga ki vah majaak nahin kar rahaa he

 'he said,' The next day we found his body hanging from a neem tree
 'shivasena ne kii sarkaar kii aalochanasheshrav ne paas do acre jameen thi or marathavada kshetra main sookhe ke kaaran uski soyabean kii fasal barbaad ho gai
 He had taken a loan of 80 thousand rupees
 iske alaava use apni beti ke vivaah kaa intjaam karne kii bhi chintaa thi

 The coming day of June 30 is officially going to be a second long, because on Tuesday our time will stop for a second
 yani aam taur par jahaan ek minute main 60 second hote hai, vahiin 30 june ko din kaa aakhri minute 61 second kaa hoga
 The US Space Science Agency NASA has confirmed this
 darasal, ek din main 86,400 second hote hai, lekin 30 june ko is samay main ek atirikt second yani lip second jud jayega
 According to Daniel mcmillan of Goddard Space Flight Center in Greenbelt, NASK, Maryland, "the Earth's rotation is slowly slowing down so it has added an extra leapsecond
" ' aisa koordinated universal time yani utisi ke mutabik he, jiskaa istemaal log dainik jivan main karte hai
 UTC is atomic time, where a period of one second is based on the predicted electromagnetic transition occurring in the atoms of the cesium
 ye transishan itane adhik vishwasaneey hote hai ki sisium clock 1,400,000 varshon tak sahi ho sakati he
 NASA released the nebayan, saying, 'earth's rotation is slowing down due to the force of gravity between the Earth, the Moon and the Sun
 'kyon joda ja rahaa he lip secondetomic or solar time main saamanjasy ke liye 1 janvari 1960 ko utisi kii vyavastha laai gai
 Since 1972, the UTC has been modified to add leap seconds if needed
 iske liye june yaa disambar main aakhri minute main ek atirikt second joda jaataa he
 The addition of additional seconds is done by the International Earth Rotation and Reference System Service
 aise main in do maap mulyon ke tulykaalan ke liye 30 june ke aakhri minute main samay ek second ke liye ruk jayega
 As soon as this happens, the last minute will be 61 seconds
 kya lip year kii tarah he lip secondalip year ke niyam ke tahat har chaar saal par calendar main ek atirikt din joda jaataa he
 This is done because the earth takes an additional time of 5 hours, 48 minutes and 46 seconds to revolve around the sun
 haalanki, isse ulat lip second kii aisi koi gananaa nahin kii ja sakati ki vah ek niyat avadhi ke baad kab joda jayega
 It depends on many things, including rotation on the Earth's own axis, mobility of the Earth's center, variations in the atmosphere, oceans, groundwater, and ice storage
